<!-- Label.stories.mdx -->

import './story.scss';
import { Canvas, Meta, Story } from '@storybook/addon-docs';

import * as Icon from './index';

<Meta title="Icons" component={Icon.SendDash} />

# Label

With `MDX`, we can define a story for `Label` right in the middle of our Markdown documentation.
